I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] S3 Content-Encoding header not persisted on objects
## Service

S3

## API Action / Feature

PutObject, GetObject, HeadObject — `Content-Encoding` header handling

## AWS Documentation

- https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/API_PutObject.html (`Content-Encoding` request header)
- https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/API_HeadObject.html (`Content-Encoding` response header)
- https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/API_GetObject.html (`Content-Encoding` response header)

## Why is this needed?

When an S3 object is uploaded with a `Content-Encoding` header (e.g., `gzip`, `application/zstd+multipart`), AWS S3 stores this metadata and returns it in subsequent `HeadObject` and `GetObject` responses. Applications use `Content-Encoding` to determine how to decode the object body.

Currently, floci receives the `Content-Encoding` header in `S3Controller.putObject()` (line 286) but only uses it for `decodeAwsChunked()` — it is **never stored** on the `S3Object` model. As a result, `HeadObject` and `GetObject` responses return `null` for `Content-Encoding`, causing `NullPointerException` in applications that expect it to be present.


## Expected behavior

```bash
# Upload object with Content-Encoding
aws s3api put-object \
  --bucket my-bucket \
  --key test.bin \
  --body test.bin \
  --content-encoding "application/zstd+multipart" \
  --content-type "application/java-aot" \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566

# HeadObject should return Content-Encoding
aws s3api head-object \
  --bucket my-bucket \
  --key test.bin \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566
# Expected: ContentEncoding: "application/zstd+multipart"

# GetObject should also return Content-Encoding
aws s3api get-object \
  --bucket my-bucket \
  --key test.bin \
  output.bin \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566
# Expected: ContentEncoding: "application/zstd+multipart" in response
```

## Actual behavior

`HeadObject` and `GetObject` responses do not include `Content-Encoding`, even when it was set during `PutObject`. The AWS SDK returns `null` for `contentEncoding()`, causing:

```
java.lang.NullPointerException: Cannot invoke "String.equals(Object)" because the return value of
"software.amazon.awssdk.services.s3.model.HeadObjectResponse.contentEncoding()" is null
```

## Root cause

In `S3Controller.java`, the `putObject` method receives `@HeaderParam("Content-Encoding") String contentEncoding` (line 286), but `s3Service.putObject()` does not accept or store it. The `S3Object` model class has no `contentEncoding` field.

## Are you willing to contribute a PR?

Yes

</pr_description>

    38	    private String acl;
    39	
    40	    public S3Object() {
    41	        this.metadata = new HashMap<>();
    42	        this.storageClass = "STANDARD";
    43	        this.checksum = new S3Checksum();
    44	        this.parts = new ArrayList<>();
    45	        this.tags = new HashMap<>();
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    public S3Object(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data, String contentType) {
    49	        this.bucketName = bucketName;
    50	        this.key = key;
    51	        this.data = data;
    52	        this.contentType = contentType != null ? contentType : "application/octet-stream";
    53	        this.size = data.length;
    54	        this.lastModified = Instant.now().truncatedTo(ChronoUnit.SECONDS);
    55	        this.eTag = computeETag(data);
    56	        this.metadata = new HashMap<>();
    57	        this.storageClass = "STANDARD";
    58	        this.checksum = new S3Checksum();
    59	        this.checksum.setChecksumSHA256(S3Checksum.sha256Base64(data));
    60	        this.checksum.setChecksumType("FULL_OBJECT");
    61	        this.parts = new ArrayList<>();
    62	        this.tags = new HashMap<>();
    63	    }

   120	    public void setAcl(String acl) { this.acl = acl; }
   121	
   122	    private static String computeETag(byte[] data) {
   123	        try {
   124	            var md = java.security.MessageDigest.getInstance("MD5");
   125	            byte[] digest = md.digest(data);
   126	            var sb = new StringBuilder("\"");
   127	            for (byte b : digest) {
   128	                sb.append(String.format("%02x", b));
   129	            }
   130	            sb.append("\"");
   131	            return sb.toString();
   132	        } catch (java.security.NoSuchAlgorithmException e) {
   133	            return "\"\"";
   134	        }
   135	    }
   136	}

   230	    private void applyObjectLock(S3Object object, Bucket bucket,
   231	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   232	        if (objectLockMode != null) {
   233	            object.setObjectLockMode(objectLockMode);
   234	            object.setRetainUntilDate(retainUntilDate);
   235	        } else if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled() && bucket.getDefaultRetention() != null) {
   236	            ObjectLockRetention def = bucket.getDefaultRetention();
   237	            object.setObjectLockMode(def.mode());
   238	            long days = "Years".equals(def.unit()) ? (long) def.value() * 365 : def.value();
   239	            object.setRetainUntilDate(Instant.now().plusSeconds(days * 86400L));
   240	        }
   241	        if (legalHoldStatus != null) {
   242	            object.setLegalHoldStatus(legalHoldStatus);
   243	        }
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    private void checkLockProtection(S3Object obj, boolean bypassGovernance) {
   247	        if ("ON".equals(obj.getLegalHoldStatus())) {
   248	            throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object has an active legal hold", 403);
   249	        }
   250	        if (obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null && Instant.now().isBefore(obj.getRetainUntilDate())) {
   251	            if ("COMPLIANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode())) {
   252	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by COMPLIANCE retention", 403);
   253	            }
   254	            if ("GOVERNANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode()) && !bypassGovernance) {
   255	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by GOVERNANCE retention", 403);
   256	            }
   257	        }
   258	    }

   298	    @PUT
   299	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   300	    public Response putObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   301	                              @PathParam("key") String key,
   302	                              @HeaderParam("Content-Type") String contentType,
   303	                              @HeaderParam("Content-Encoding") String contentEncoding,
   304	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-content-sha256") String contentSha256,

   353	            }

   355	            return resp.build();
   356	        } catch (AwsException e) {

   426	    private Response handleRangeRequest(S3Object obj, String rangeHeader) {
   427	        byte[] data = obj.getData();
   428	        int totalSize = data.length;
   429	        String rangeSpec = rangeHeader.substring("bytes=".length()).trim();
   430	
   431	        int start, end;
   432	        try {
   433	            int dash = rangeSpec.indexOf('-');
   434	            if (dash < 0) {
   435	                return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   436	            }
   437	            String before = rangeSpec.substring(0, dash);
   438	            String after = rangeSpec.substring(dash + 1);
   439	            if (before.isEmpty() && after.isEmpty()) {
   440	                return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   441	            }
   442	            if (before.isEmpty()) {
   443	                int suffix = Integer.parseInt(after);
   444	                if (suffix <= 0) {
   445	                    return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   446	                }
   447	                start = Math.max(0, totalSize - suffix);
   448	                end = totalSize - 1;
   449	            } else {
   450	                start = Integer.parseInt(before);
   451	                end = after.isEmpty() ? totalSize - 1 : Math.min(Integer.parseInt(after), totalSize - 1);
   452	            }
   453	        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
   454	            return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   455	        }
   456	
   457	        if (start < 0 || start >= totalSize || start > end) {
   458	            return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   459	        }
   460	
   461	        byte[] rangeData = java.util.Arrays.copyOfRange(data, start, end + 1);
   462	        return Response.status(206)
   463	                .entity(rangeData)
   464	                .header("Content-Type", obj.getContentType())
   465	                .header("Content-Length", rangeData.length)
   466	                .header("Content-Range", "bytes " + start + "-" + end + "/" + totalSize)
   467	                .header("ETag", obj.getETag())
   468	                .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   469	                .header("Accept-Ranges", "bytes")
   470	                .build();
   471	    }
   472	
   473	    private Response invalidRangeResponse(int totalSize) {
   474	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
   475	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   476	                .start("Error")
   477	                .elem("Code", "InvalidRange")
   478	                .elem("Message", "The requested range is not satisfiable.")
   479	                .elem("RequestId", java.util.UUID.randomUUID().toString())
   480	                .end("Error")
   481	                .build();
   482	        return Response.status(416)
   483	                .entity(xml)
   484	                .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   485	                .header("Content-Range", "bytes */" + totalSize)
   486	                .build();
   487	    }

   826	    // --- AWS Chunked Decoding ---
   827	
   828	    /**
   829	     * Decodes aws-chunked transfer encoding used by AWS SDK v2 with SigV4 chunk signing.
   830	     * Format: hex-size;chunk-signature=sig\r\n data \r\n ... 0;chunk-signature=sig\r\n
   831	     */
   832	    private byte[] decodeAwsChunked(byte[] body, String contentEncoding, String contentSha256) {
   833	        boolean isAwsChunked = (contentEncoding != null && contentEncoding.contains("aws-chunked"))
   834	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD".equals(contentSha256)
   835	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD-TRAILER".equals(contentSha256);
   836	        if (!isAwsChunked) {
   837	            return body;
   838	        }
   839	
   840	        try {
   841	            ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   842	            String raw = new String(body, StandardCharsets.ISO_8859_1);
   843	            int pos = 0;
   844	            while (pos < raw.length()) {
   845	                int lineEnd = raw.indexOf('\n', pos);
   846	                if (lineEnd < 0) break;
   847	                String line = raw.substring(pos, lineEnd).trim();
   848	                int semiColon = line.indexOf(';');
   849	                String hexSize = semiColon >= 0 ? line.substring(0, semiColon) : line;
   850	                int chunkSize = Integer.parseInt(hexSize.trim(), 16);
   851	                if (chunkSize == 0) break;
   852	
   853	                int dataStart = lineEnd + 1;
   854	                byte[] chunkData = new byte[chunkSize];
   855	                System.arraycopy(body, dataStart, chunkData, 0, chunkSize);
   856	                out.write(chunkData);
   857	
   858	                pos = dataStart + chunkSize;
   859	                if (pos < raw.length() && raw.charAt(pos) == '\r') pos++;

   462	                               String destBucket, String destKey,
   463	                               String metadataDirective, Map<String, String> replacementMetadata,
   464	                               String storageClass, String contentType) {
   465	        S3Object source = getObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey);
   466	        ensureBucketExists(destBucket);
   467	
   468	        boolean replaceMetadata = "REPLACE".equalsIgnoreCase(metadataDirective);
   469	        Map<String, String> metadata = replaceMetadata ? new LinkedHashMap<>() : new LinkedHashMap<>(source.getMetadata());

   471	            metadata.putAll(replacementMetadata);
   472	        }
   473

   475	        String effectiveStorageClass = storageClass != null ? storageClass : source.getStorageClass();
   476	        S3Object copy = storeObject(destBucket, destKey, source.getData(), effectiveContentType, metadata,
   477	                effectiveStorageClass, source.getChecksum(), source.getParts(), null, null, null);
   478	        copy.setETag(source.getETag());
   479	        LOG.debugv("Copied object: {0}/{1} -> {2}/{3}", sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey);
   480	        fireNotifications(destBucket, destKey, "ObjectCreated:Copy", copy);
   481	        return copy;
   482	    }

   789	    public S3Object completeMultipartUpload(String bucket, String key, String uploadId, List<Integer> partNumbers) {
   790	        MultipartUpload upload = multipartUploads.get(uploadId);
   791	        if (upload == null || !upload.getBucket().equals(bucket) || !upload.getKey().equals(key)) {
   792	            throw new AwsException("NoSuchUpload",
   793	                    "The specified multipart upload does not exist.", 404);
   794	        }
   795	
   796	        // Verify all requested parts exist
   797	        for (int num : partNumbers) {
   798	            if (!upload.getParts().containsKey(num)) {
   799	                throw new AwsException("InvalidPart",
   800	                        "One or more of the specified parts could not be found. Part " + num + " is missing.", 400);
   801	            }
   802	        }
   803	
   804	        // Concatenate parts in order
   805	        try {
   806	            ByteArrayOutputStream combined = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   807	            MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("MD5");
   808	
   809	            for (int num : partNumbers) {
   810	                byte[] partData = inMemory
   811	                        ? memoryMultipartStore.get(uploadId).get(num)
   812	                        : Files.readAllBytes(dataRoot.resolve(".multipart").resolve(uploadId).resolve(String.valueOf(num)));
   813	                combined.write(partData);
   814	                // For composite ETag: hash each part's MD5
   815	                md.update(computeETagBytes(partData));
   816	            }
   817	
   818	            byte[] allData = combined.toByteArray();
   819	
   820	            // Composite ETag: MD5 of concatenated part MD5s, suffixed with part count
   821	            String compositeETag = "\"" + bytesToHex(md.digest()) + "-" + partNumbers.size() + "\"";
   822	
   823	            List<Part> completedParts = partNumbers.stream()
   824	                    .map(num -> copyPart(upload.getParts().get(num)))
   825	                    .toList();
   826	            S3Checksum checksum = buildChecksum(allData, completedParts, true);
   827	            S3Object object = storeObject(bucket, key, allData, upload.getContentType(), upload.getMetadata(),
   828	                    upload.getStorageClass(), checksum, completedParts, null, null, null);
   829	            // Override the ETag with the composite multipart ETag
   830	            object.setETag(compositeETag);
   831	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucket, key), object);
   832

   834	            cleanupMultipart(uploadId);

import io.quarkus.test.junit.QuarkusTest;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.MethodOrderer;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Order;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.TestMethodOrder;

import java.util.Arrays;

import static org.hamcrest.Matchers.*;

@QuarkusTest
@TestMethodOrder(MethodOrderer.OrderAnnotation.class)
class S3IntegrationTest {

    @Test
    @Order(1)
    void createBucket() {
        given()
        .when()
            .put("/test-bucket")
        .then()
            .statusCode(200)
            .header("Location", equalTo("/test-bucket"));
    }

    @Test
    @Order(2)
    void createDuplicateBucketFails() {
        given()
        .when()
            .put("/test-bucket")
        .then()
            .statusCode(409)
            .body(containsString("BucketAlreadyOwnedByYou"));
    }

    @Test
    @Order(3)
    void listBuckets() {
        given()
        .when()
            .get("/")
        .then()
            .statusCode(200)
            .body(containsString("test-bucket"));
    }

    @Test
    @Order(4)
    void putObject() {
        given()
            .contentType("text/plain")
            .header("x-amz-meta-owner", "team-a")
            .header("x-amz-storage-class", "STANDARD_IA")
            .body("Hello World from S3!")
        .when()
            .put("/test-bucket/greeting.txt")
        .then()
            .statusCode(200)
            .header("ETag", notNullValue());
    }

    @Test
    @Order(5)
    void getObject() {
        given()
        .when()
            .get("/test-bucket/greeting.txt")
        .then()
            .statusCode(200)
            .header("ETag", notNullValue())
            .header("Content-Length", notNullValue())
            .header("x-amz-meta-owner", equalTo("team-a"))
            .header("x-amz-storage-class", equalTo("STANDARD_IA"))
            .header("x-amz-checksum-sha256", notNullValue())
            .body(equalTo("Hello World from S3!"));
    }

    @Test
    @Order(6)
    void getObjectAttributes() {
        given()
            .header("x-amz-object-attributes", "ETag,ObjectSize,StorageClass,Checksum")
        .when()
            .get("/test-bucket/greeting.txt?attributes")
        .then()
            .statusCode(200)
            .body(containsString("<GetObjectAttributesResponse"))
            .body(containsString("<StorageClass>STANDARD_IA</StorageClass>"))
            .body(containsString("<ObjectSize>20</ObjectSize>"))
            .body(containsString("<ChecksumSHA256>"));
    }

    @Test
    @Order(7)
    void headObject() {
        given()
        .when()
            .head("/test-bucket/greeting.txt")
        .then()
            .statusCode(200)
            .header("ETag", notNullValue())
            .header("Content-Length", notNullValue())
            .header("x-amz-meta-owner", equalTo("team-a"))
            .header("x-amz-storage-class", equalTo("STANDARD_IA"))
            .header("x-amz-checksum-sha256", notNullValue());
    }

        .then()
            .statusCode(404)
            .body(containsString("NoSuchKey"));

cat > /tmp/repro_s3_content_encoding.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
TEST_FILE=src/test/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/services/s3/S3ContentEncodingReproTest.java
cat > "$TEST_FILE" <<'JAVA'
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.s3;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.s3.model.S3Object;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.io.TempDir;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Map;

import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals;

class S3ContentEncodingReproTest {
    @TempDir
    Path tempDir;

    @Test
    void putObjectPersistsContentEncodingMetadata() {
        S3Service s3 = new S3Service(new InMemoryStorage<>(), new InMemoryStorage<>(), tempDir.resolve("s3"), false);
        s3.createBucket("bucket", null);
        S3Object put = s3.putObject("bucket", "key", "payload".getBytes(), "application/java-aot", Map.of(), "STANDARD", "application/zstd+multipart", null, null, null);
        assertEquals("application/zstd+multipart", put.getContentEncoding());
        assertEquals("application/zstd+multipart", s3.headObject("bucket", "key").getContentEncoding());
        assertEquals("application/zstd+multipart", s3.getObject("bucket", "key").getContentEncoding());
    }
}
JAVA
trap 'rm -f "$TEST_FILE"' EXIT
./mvnw -q -Dtest=S3ContentEncodingReproTest test
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_s3_content_encoding.sh

   834	    private byte[] decodeAwsChunked(byte[] body, String contentEncoding, String contentSha256) {
   835	        boolean isAwsChunked = (contentEncoding != null && contentEncoding.contains("aws-chunked"))
   836	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD".equals(contentSha256)
   837	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD-TRAILER".equals(contentSha256);
   838	        if (!isAwsChunked) {
   839	            return body;
   840	        }
   841	
   842	        try {
   843	            ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   844	            String raw = new String(body, StandardCharsets.ISO_8859_1);
   845	            int pos = 0;
   846	            while (pos < raw.length()) {
   847	                int lineEnd = raw.indexOf('\n', pos);
   848	                if (lineEnd < 0) break;
   849	                String line = raw.substring(pos, lineEnd).trim();
   850	                int semiColon = line.indexOf(';');
   851	                String hexSize = semiColon >= 0 ? line.substring(0, semiColon) : line;
   852	                int chunkSize = Integer.parseInt(hexSize.trim(), 16);
   853	                if (chunkSize == 0) break;
   854	
   855	                int dataStart = lineEnd + 1;
   856	                byte[] chunkData = new byte[chunkSize];
   857	                System.arraycopy(body, dataStart, chunkData, 0, chunkSize);
   858	                out.write(chunkData);
   859	
   860	                pos = dataStart + chunkSize;
   861	                if (pos < raw.length() && raw.charAt(pos) == '\r') pos++;
   862	                if (pos < raw.length() && raw.charAt(pos) == '\n') pos++;
   863	            }
   864	            return out.toByteArray();

   867	        if (contentEncoding == null) {
   868	            return null;

   873	                .filter(encoding -> !"aws-chunked".equalsIgnoreCase(encoding))

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.s3;

import io.quarkus.test.junit.QuarkusTest;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;

import static io.restassured.RestAssured.given;
import static org.hamcrest.Matchers.equalTo;

@QuarkusTest
class S3ContentEncodingHttpReproTest {
    @Test
    void contentEncodingIsReturnedFromHeadAndGet() {
        given().when().put("/encoding-repro-bucket").then().statusCode(200);

        given()
                .contentType("application/java-aot")
                .header("Content-Encoding", "application/zstd+multipart")
                .body("payload")
        .when()
                .put("/encoding-repro-bucket/test.bin")
        .then()
                .statusCode(200);

        given()
        .when()
                .head("/encoding-repro-bucket/test.bin")
        .then()
                .statusCode(200)
                .header("Content-Encoding", equalTo("application/zstd+multipart"));

        given()
        .when()
                .get("/encoding-repro-bucket/test.bin")
        .then()
                .statusCode(200)
                .header("Content-Encoding", equalTo("application/zstd+multipart"))
                .body(equalTo("payload"));
    }
}
JAVA
trap 'rm -f "$TEST_FILE"' EXIT
./mvnw -q -Dmaven.compiler.release=21 -Dtest=S3ContentEncodingHttpReproTest test
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_s3_content_encoding_http.sh
